 According to the India Today - Axis My India exit poll, the BJP may lose power in the state of Jharkhand
 agsit pole ke anumaan bataa rahe hai ki jharkhand vidhansabha chunaav main vipakshi gathbandhan nirnaayak jeet hasil karne ja rahaa he
 This opposition coalition consists of Jharkhand Mukti Morcha (JMM), Congress and Rashtriya Janata Dal (RJD)
 paanch charnon vaale jharkhand vidhansabha chunaav main is baar bijepi ne akele taal thoki thi
 In the 81-member house, BJP may win 22 to 32 seats according to exit poll estimates
 vahiin vipakshi gathbandhan kii jholii main 38 se 50 seat ja sakati he
 The magic figure of the majority in the Jharkhand assembly is 41
 abhi tak jharkhand vidhansabha main bijepi ke paas 37 seat thim, vahiin uske sahyogi rahe aal jharkhand students union (AJSU) ke paas 5 seat thim
 In the 2014 assembly elections, JMM won 19 seats, Congress 6 and Babulal Marandi-led party Jharkhand Vikas Morcha i
e
 JVM won 8 seats
 baad main JVM ke 6 vidhayakon ne bijepi ko samarthan dekar paala badal liya
 Others also won 6 seats in the 2014 assembly
 2019 vidhansabha chunaav ke liye rajya main bijepi or AJSU ne alag alag chunaav ladaa
 The exit poll estimates are a big setback for the BJP as the BJP won 11 out of 14 seats in the Lok Sabha elections in May this year
 2019 loksabhaa chunaav se jharkhand vidhansabha siton kaa akalan kiya jaae to may main rajya main bijepi ko 57 seat par badhat hasil thi
 According to India Today - Axis My India poll, the three major parties of the opposition alliance have performed better in this election than in 2014
 JMM ko 2014 main jiti 19 siton kii tulana main is baar 24 se 28 seat par jeet hasil ho sakati he
 At the same time, the figure of Congress seats can also be 12 to 18 seats this time
 2014 main congress ko sirf 6 seat par hi jeet hasil hui thi
 The RJD, which is part of the opposition alliance, may win 2 to 4 seats this time
 2014 vidhansabha chunaav main RJD kaa khaataa bhi nahin khul sakaa tha
 Vote Share As far as the vote share is concerned, bjp's vote share can increase by 3% compared to 2014 assembly elections
 bijepi ko is baar 34% vot milane kaa anumaan he
 But when it comes to seats, BJP may have to beat the opposition alliance this time
 jatigat ganit kii baat kii jaae to jmm-congress-rjd gathbandhan ko ST votaron main se 53% or isai votaron main se 69% kaa samarthan mil rahaa he
 At the same time, BJP could get support of 27% in SC and 12% in Christian voters
